<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstandelijk.html>afstandelijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">standoffish, aloof, distant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-hood, -ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the former component derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstand.html>afstand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">distance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and the suffix <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstandelijkheid.html>afstandelijkheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>aloofness, standoffishness</li>
<li>detachment</li></ol>

***afstrijken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afstrijken.html>afstrijken</a> (109869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">afstriken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:strijken.html>strijken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstrijken.html>afstrijken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a match, to attempt to ignite it</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> veiligheidslucifer, in tegensteling <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> strijklucifer, <a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:redelijk.html>redelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:afstrijken.html>afstrijken</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A safety match, as opposed to a strike-anywhere match, can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> be easily <b>struck</b> on any surface.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <span class="Latn" lang="en">rub out</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aftakeling.html>aftakeling</a> (44181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aftakelen.html>aftakelen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.

<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">decrepitude</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">decay</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">decline</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in physical or mental condition</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aftrap.html>aftrap</a> (23596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aftrap.html>aftrappen</a></i>.  Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">off</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">kick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kickoff</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:aftreden.html>aftreden</a></i>. ***aftrekken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aftrekken.html>aftrekken</a> (9152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aftrecken</i>. The sense “to subtract” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_Stevin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Simon Stevin"><a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> Stevin</a> as a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dētrahō</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trekken.html>trekken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aftrekken.html>aftrekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> arithmetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subtract</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to clean/level etc. with a squeegee</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wank, to <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> off; to stimulate with one's hand of one's own or another one's <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afval.html>afval</a></i>, shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slachtafval</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">that which fell off from slaughtered meat.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">offal</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afvallen.html>afvallen</a> (11520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afvallen.html>afvallen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afvallen.html>afvallen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose weight, <a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a> down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop out, to no longer be able to partake</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to renounce, to renege, to lose loyalty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dispute, to go against (a person)</li></ol>

</p>
